 kendriya cabinet ne buudhvaar ko sarogesi regulation bill 2016 ko manjuuri de di
 The Bill provides for the protection of the rights of surrogacy or surrogate mother and to give legal recognition to the parents of such children
 nahin ho sakegi vyavsaayik sarogeseis bill ke sansad main paas hone ke baad vyavsaayik yani paise ke liesrogesinhin kii ja sakati sirf jaruratmand banjh danpatiyon ke liye hi naitik rup se saroget maa banane kii manjuuri hogi
 There has been an all-round debate on this decision of the government, in which questions are being raised whether the decision is the ideology or thinking of the government or the need of society
 garib mahilaon kii kokh kiraye par lene kaa chalan hoga bandakendriya mantri sushamaa swaraj ne kaha bill ke paksh main daleel dete hue kaha kii is bill se paise ke liye garib mahila kii kokh kiraye par lene kaa chalan band hoga or saroget child ko wo tamaam adhikaar honge jo biological child ko hote hai
 He said that the segregation of serogacy is being done in an unethical manner which has to be stopped and the new bill will help in that
 sushamaa swaraj ne kaha ki jarurat ke liye shuru kii gai sarogesi kii suvidha ab shauk ban gai he or jo celebrity sirf apni patni ko dard se bachaane ke liye iskaa istemaal kar rahe hai unhen sochna hoga
 Surrogacy Board will be constituted so that the Surrogacy Board will be set up at the central level, also in the states and union territories so that new laws can be properly followed
 ye bill narendra modi sarkaar kii ek badi uplabdhi kha ja saktaa he jise agle sansad satr main pesh kiya jayega
 The argument that the government has made in favor of the bill is that India was being called a 'surrogacy hub' for the last few years
 kyonki yahaan kam kharch main kiraye kii kokh mil jaati thi
 Rural and tribal women were being particularly exploited
 pichhali sarkaron ne 11 baar sansad main is bill ko pesh karne kaa vaada kiya lekin ise puraa nahin kiya
 Who will not be able to take surrogacy? Single parent, live-in couples, homosexual couples and unmarried couples
 kinhen milegaa phayda?jis kapal kii kanoonee taur shaadi hui ho or shaadi ke paanch saal baad bhi baccha nahin hua ho
 In such a couple, the age of the wife should be between 23 to 50 and the age of the husband between 26 and 55 years
 koun ban sakegi saroget madar?wo mahila jo kapal kii kareebi rishtedaar ho, vah ek hi baar saroget madar ban sakati he
 a woman who becomes a surrogate mother must be married and already a mother of a healthy child
 niyam todane par sajaa kaa praavdhansarogesi ke nae niyam todane par 10 saal tak kaid or 10 lakh rupye tak kaa jurmaana hoga
